posted:Posted December 26, 2023
msg:We spent Cristmas Day at the Intercontinental Dameisha in Shenzhen. A 40 minute Didi drive from Futian and the hotel has a private beach.. The hotel is modern and lovely. Check in was quick and smooth with an English speaking front desk.  We received two complimentary breakfasts from the hotel. The breakfast is a mix of Western style and Chinese and was delicious - definitely reccommended. The rooms were comfy with a complimentary fruit bowl and lots of drinking water in the room. To my surprise the TV channels featured many English channel options. The beds were soft and comfortable, had a lovely bathroom and a small but nice balcony overlooking the sea and pool. The hotel also sports a fitness room, saunas and an indoor swimming pool, a childrens' playroom and more. It is also conveniently close to the Outlet store village. We had a pleasant stay. Only down side was that there weren't many Western restaurant options to choose from in the village, but if you don't mind Burger King, Macdonalds and Pizza Hut, you'll be fine. You can also eat at the hotel and be sure of a lovely meal at their restaurant.

info:Deluxe Sea-view Room

info:5 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted November 3, 2023
msg:I have done a lot of travelling over the years and to many countries and hundreds of hotels in China and the location of this hotel and their private beach is spectacular.

We have stayed here a couple of times and have decided that we will make it an annual event or even twice a year.

We booked Seaview room and included Breakfast and buffet dinner for both days. The buffet is amongst the best you will find in any 5 start hotel in the world and one of the few that I can actually eat a huge variety of food until I cannot move, most buffet dinners my wife and I just have a nibble and that is usually it.

The breakfast is also first class, a big variety of different food and you can actually eat it and enjoy it. Again we also had very long breakfast overlooking the ocean and mountains.

I recommend it to anyone that want true 5 star service, Amazing Views and Great Food.

My only critisism is that as this is not a new hotel and while maintained in general very good, we did see mild on the curtains in the bathroom and ocean view curtains and that is absolutely not a good thing. Apart from that we are looking forward to our next stay that will probably be after the China New Year Holiday.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe Room - Sea-View (Upper floor)
info:Stayed in April 2022
info:Friends
info:21 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted July 4, 2022
msg:The hotel is in a good location at Dameisha, about 45min from downtown Shenzhen. Rooms were nice, spacious and clean. It's a good get away from Shenzhen. The pool and the beach is the best part of the hotel, but beware that this is also very popular for families with kids. Check in was very slow given the masses of people showing up at the same time and house keeping also couldn't keep up. I didn't get my room until after after 3:30pm. 

The food was fine. However, the dinner buffet was pricey and not worth the value. The main restaurant could definitely be improved upon. My friends and I ended up ordering delivery for food instead. Service was hindered by the masses of families. 

The pool would be a lot better if they strictly enforced the part of the pool where the bar is to be adults only. This is partially done as the water slide and kids friendly amenities are at the other end of the pool. But having an adults only area would be better for everyone. The bar at the pool was also very very slow with their service and I ended up just getting beers as it was the fastest option.  

It's a good get away from Shenzhen, I would recommend. But just be prepared for masses of families with children. Definitely a kids friendly hotel, with lots of amenities catered for them.

I already told you that I paid 100 yuan for breakfast at the front desk yesterday, but the waiter didn't believe it. I kept repeating that I couldn't have breakfast without paying. I was very angry because it was about 9:30 to 9:45 in the morning. At that time, it was the busy time for breakfast in the hotel and there were many people in the restaurant at that time.

The waiter kept repeating that I didn't pay and I couldn't have breakfast. This made me feel embarrassed and humiliated because many customers were looking at me. It made me feel bad because the male waiter kept repeating that I didn't pay and I couldn't. Have breakfast and let other guests believe so too.

Then, the male waiter went too far and asked me to take the elevator to the hotel lobby and find a staff member at the front desk to confirm that I had paid for breakfast before I could come to the restaurant for breakfast. This was too much.

After that, I was super angry. I told the male waiter that you should call the manager or the front desk staff in the lobby. I will not go to the lobby to find the staff because I was not wrong. I really paid. I also paid the hotel on May 8. After the payment was made, Alipay receipts for a total of 3,000 yuan were given to the male staff, but the male staff insisted not to believe me and refused to give me breakfast.

I think this is too much and makes me humiliated in public. The hotel management should provide more training and education so that employees know how to handle crises and solve problems when they encounter them, instead of making guests humiliated and unhappy.

In fact, the male staff can politely say to the guest first, "Sorry, we can't check your payment information. Are you willing to pay for breakfast?"

Alternatively, it can be deducted from the deposit. You should first ask the guests to sit down and talk slowly, not to ask them to stand and talk, because standing in the center of the road, the distance between the platforms is also very close. At that time, the guests next to them are also watching and listening, which makes I am uncomfortable.

After that, I insisted on asking the male staff to confirm with the front desk. After confirming, he said that the front desk said that you paid for breakfast, but because the system has not been updated, there is no record.

Then I said that I checked in at 2 pm yesterday and the record was not updated until 9 am the next morning. This was too much. After that, I went to get food, but I couldn't eat it. I put food in my mouth and couldn't swallow it.

Then, I changed to a room on the club side. Kelly, the housekeeper, was very nice and attentive. He helped me arrange for a waiter to pick up my luggage and find a car to take me to the club. After arriving at the club, Kelly also came out to pick me up. After registering, Kelly sent me there. She gave me a gift, which included a cup and aromatherapy stones. I was very happy because Kelly still remembered the last time I stayed at the club and asked her about turn-down products and whether there were any scented candles that could help me fall asleep.

Kelly actually remembered that I like scented items, which was so attentive and surprised me. After registering, I said that I was unhappy about breakfast and had a stomachache. Kelly also asked the restaurant to bring me hot milk to warm my stomach. It was so comforting. Afterwards, after arriving in the room, take stomach medicine and wait two hours until your stomach pain is gone before you can go swimming.

Therefore, I hope that in the main hotel building, staff training and crisis management can be strengthened and the hotel staff can be taught how to treat guests and have a friendly smile, so that guests can enjoy themselves and feel at home when they come to the hotel. More guests choose this hotel for their vacation.

Finally, I hope that when the hotel management meets, they should discuss how to improve the morale and sense of belonging of hotel staff, and establish a reward and punishment system so that frontline staff can work harder and improve service quality. For example, the Best Service Employee Award and the Best Goodwill Ambassador Employee Award are set up so that employees with the best service can serve as good examples for other employees. At the same time, cash rewards and a good promotion system are also set up to improve employee morale and make them more positive. Put in the work and provide better and quality service to guests.

Finally, I feel very much that Kelly Bai, the club's butler, provides me with good, attentive and high-quality services every time I stay.

I hope the hotel will cherish this employee and other employees will follow her example. I hope to see Kelly promoted in the near future, because Club InterContinental is a blessing to the hotel to have such an excellent employee.

msg:My family and I went to the InterContinental Shenzhen Dameisha Resort and had an unforgettable vacation. This hotel is located on the Dameisha beachfront in eastern Shenzhen, facing the South China Sea and surrounded by mountains on three sides. It has beautiful scenery and a quiet environment. The design and decoration of the hotel are very high-end, and the rooms are spacious and comfortable. Each room has a large balcony where you can enjoy sea views and sunrise and sunset.

The room we stayed in had a king-sized double bed and a spacious bathroom. The decoration of the room is very tasteful, with soft colors and makes people feel very relaxed. There is a deck chair on the balcony with a platform. It is very romantic to sit and listen to the waves and look at the stars.

The hotel's dining is also very good, with four restaurants and bars offering Chinese, Western, Italian and Asian cuisine. The buffet breakfast there is very rich, with a variety of breads, biscuits, fruits, freshly squeezed juices, coffee, tea, milk, yogurt, cereals, ham, bacon, sausages, eggs, porridge, noodles, pancakes, waffles, honey, Jam and more.

The hotel's recreational facilities are also complete, including an outdoor swimming pool, an indoor swimming pool, a children's playground, a fitness center, a sauna and steam room, and a SPA center. Go swimming, play in the water, play sports and relax. The hotel also has a private beach with fine sand and clear water. We can bask in the sun, play in the sand and take photos there, which is very fun.

The service in the hotel is also very good. The staff are friendly, enthusiastic, professional and responsive to all requests. Our check-in and check-out went smoothly without any problems. The hotel also provides free parking. We feel that the hotel is very cost-effective and value for money.

All in all, we had a very enjoyable vacation at the InterContinental Shenzhen Dameisha Resort and experienced the luxurious resort lifestyle. We highly recommend this hotel and hope to come back again.

The room is fully equipped, but the shower drain is higher than the ground, and water accumulates as soon as the faucet is turned on.

The breakfast is rich in variety and the service staff is very enthusiastic, but the quality is average, with few Western options and mostly Chinese options. But it was a little uncomfortable when a staff member asked me to write a positive review on Dianping during breakfast.

Overall, it's a great hotel.
